logo: 10 Minute School

Summary : This is the official logo of "10 Minute School", an educational platform.

Logo Elements :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" on the left, with the "0" partially encircled by a red arrow forming the upper right quadrant.
  тАв To the right of the number, the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" are stacked, with "MINUTE" above "SCHOOL", both in uppercase sans-serif font.
  тАв The "1" and "0" are bold and black, with the red arrow providing a contrasting accent.
  тАв The overall design is horizontal, with the text aligned to the right of the numeric element.

Dimensions & Placement :
  тАв The "10" is approximately the same height as the stacked text.
  тАв The red arrow starts at the left side of the "0" and curves clockwise to the top.

Analysis :
  тАв The use of a red arrow in the "0" suggests movement or the passage of time, reinforcing the "minute" concept.
  тАв The clean, modern font and minimal colour palette (black and red) convey professionalism and clarity, suitable for an educational brand. <!-- figure, from page 0 (l=0.403,t=0.133,r=0.599,b=0.182), with ID c70ea80a-a585-4629-a9db-5819e9704d42 -->

Summary : This is a logo for an online batch program targeting HSC 2026 students, with a focus on Bangla, English, and ICT subjects.

Logo Elements :
  тАв Main text: "HSC 26" in white font on a red background.
  тАв Secondary text: "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch in Bengali) in bold black Bengali script, with a wireless signal icon to the right.

  тАв All text is centered and uses a combination of Bengali and English.
  тАв The design uses red, black, and white as primary colors.

Dimensions & Placement :
  тАв Rectangular layout, with the main "HSC 26" block at the top, followed by the larger "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" text, and the subject list at the bottom.
  тАв Wireless signal icon is placed to the right of the main Bengali text.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo is designed to be bold and easily recognizable, using high-contrast colors and clear subject focus.
  тАв The wireless icon emphasizes the online nature of the batch.
  тАв The use of both Bengali and English text targets a bilingual audience. <!-- figure, from page 1 (l=0.064,t=0.028,r=0.201,b=0.074), with ID ff10e082-4052-4030-9b35-36fc6c52ff4c -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text and Design :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" in bold black font, with the "0" partially formed by a red arrow curving to the right.
  тАв To the right of the "10", the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines ("MINUTE" above "SCHOOL").
  тАв The red arrow within the "0" is the only colored element, drawing attention to the number and suggesting movement or progress.
  тАв The overall design is horizontal, with the text aligned to the right of the numeric/graphic element.

Dimensions and Placement :
  тАв The "10" (with arrow) is approximately square in height, matching the combined height of the two text lines.
  тАв The logo is designed for clear horizontal placement, suitable for website headers or branding materials.

Analysis :
  тАв The use of a red arrow within the "0" visually emphasizes the concept of time and quick progress, aligning with the "10 Minute School" brand identity focused on fast, efficient learning. <!-- figure, from page 2 (l=0.801,t=0.035,r=0.932,b=0.069), with ID 3ebb52c9-4b08-4459-8e99-a4f3350dabb3 -->

logo: HSC 26 ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ  
Main Text : 
  тАв "HSC 26" in bold white text on a red background.
  тАв "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch in Bengali) in bold black text.
  тАв Wi-Fi signal icon to the right of the main text, indicating online connectivity.

  тАв "ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ ┬╖ ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ ┬╖ ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐" (Bangla ┬╖ English ┬╖ ICT) in white text on a red background, denoting the subjects included.

Design & Layout : 
  тАв Rectangular, horizontally stacked layout.
  тАв Red, black, and white colour scheme.
  тАв All text is in bold, with clear separation between main and subtext.

  тАв The logo uses strong, contrasting colours and a Wi-Fi icon to emphasise its online educational focus for HSC 2026 students, specifically in Bangla, English, and ICT. <!-- figure, from page 3 (l=0.066,t=0.028,r=0.199,b=0.074), with ID 91788bce-f5c5-4665-ae7d-0f47f3b1c83a -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text & Design :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" in bold black font, with the "0" partially open and containing a red arrow curving clockwise inside it.
  тАв To the right of the "10", the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines: "MINUTE" on top, "SCHOOL" below.
  тАв The red arrow within the "0" visually suggests the concept of time or a clock, reinforcing the "minute" theme.

Dimensions & Placement :
  тАв The "10" is larger and positioned to the left, with "MINUTE SCHOOL" aligned vertically to its right.
  тАв The red arrow is centered within the "0" and points upward and to the right.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses a bold, modern typeface and a red accent to draw attention to the time-based theme.

Summary : This is a logo for an online educational batch targeting HSC 2026 students, with text in both English and Bengali indicating subjects covered.

logo: HSC 26 Online Batch (ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛, ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐, ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐)
  Text Elements : 
    тАв "HSC 26" in bold white text on a red background.
    тАв "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch in Bengali) in bold black text with a Wi-Fi signal icon.
    тАв "ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ ┬╖ ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ ┬╖ ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐" (Bangla ┬╖ English ┬╖ ICT) in white text on a red background.
  Design & Layout : 
    тАв Rectangular, horizontally stacked text blocks.
    тАв Red, black, and white colour scheme.
    тАв Wi-Fi signal icon to the right of the main Bengali text.
    тАв All-caps and bold fonts for emphasis.
  Dimensions & Placement : 
    тАв Central alignment of all text.
    тАв Wi-Fi icon placed at the upper right of the main Bengali text block.
  Analysis : 
    тАв The logo is designed to attract HSC 2026 students for online classes in Bangla, English, and ICT, using bold colours and clear subject emphasis for visibility and recognition. <!-- figure, from page 7 (l=0.065,t=0.029,r=0.198,b=0.074), with ID 290e012b-01c8-41de-800f-5e73207f6774 -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text and Design :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" in bold black font, with the "0" partially open and containing a red arrow curving clockwise inside it.
  тАв To the right of the number, the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines.
  тАв The design is simple, with a modern sans-serif typeface and a red accent for the arrow.

Dimensions and Placement :
  тАв The "10" is on the left, with "MINUTE" on the top right and "SCHOOL" directly below it.
  тАв The red arrow is integrated into the "0" of "10", pointing to the right.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses a red arrow to suggest speed or progress, reinforcing the "10 Minute" concept of quick learning.
  тАв The clean, bold design and use of black and red create a strong, memorable brand identity. <!-- figure, from page 7 (l=0.801,t=0.034,r=0.932,b=0.069), with ID df0bfc38-10f0-429f-a2ea-025ee75ff4a1 -->

  тАв Rectangular logo with a red and white color scheme.
  тАв "HSC 26" in bold white text on a red background at the top.
  тАв "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch) in large black Bengali script below, with a stylized wireless signal icon to the right.

  тАв All text is horizontally aligned and centered.

  тАв The logo is designed to promote an online batch for HSC 2026 students, focusing on Bangla, English, and ICT subjects. logo: 10 Minute School

Scene Overview : 
  тАв The image is a logo for "10 Minute School".
  тАв The design features a large, bold "10" on the left, with the "0" partially open and containing a red arrow forming part of the zero.
  тАв To the right, the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" are stacked in uppercase, sans-serif font.
  тАв The overall colour palette is black for the text and a single red accent for the arrow.

Technical Details : 
  тАв No additional text, taglines, or UI elements are present.
  тАв The logo is on a white background.

Spatial Relationships : 
  тАв The "10" is left-aligned, with "MINUTE SCHOOL" right-aligned and stacked in two lines.
  тАв The red arrow is positioned within the "0" of "10", pointing upward and to the right.

  тАв To the right of the "10", the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines: "MINUTE" on top, "SCHOOL" below.
  тАв The font is modern and sans-serif.
  тАв The background is white.

Dimensions and Placement :
  тАв The "10" is on the left, with the text "MINUTE SCHOOL" aligned to the right.
  тАв The red arrow is integrated into the "0" of "10", making it visually distinctive.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses a bold, modern design to emphasize quick learning ("10 Minute") and education ("School").
  тАв The red arrow suggests movement, progress, or the passage of time, reinforcing the "minute" concept. <!-- figure, from page 15 (l=0.801,t=0.034,r=0.932,b=0.069), with ID 9b81242b-30e8-41a7-911f-ed11d275053c -->

Summary : This is a logo for an online educational batch targeting HSC 2026 students, with a focus on Bangla, English, and ICT subjects.

logo: HSC 26 Online Batch (Bangla, English, ICT)
  Main Text Elements :
    тАв "HSC 26" in bold white text on a red background.
    тАв "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch in Bengali) in bold black text.
    тАв "ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ тАв ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ тАв ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐" (Bangla тАв English тАв ICT) in white text on a red background.
    тАв Wi-Fi signal icon to the right of the main text, indicating online/remote learning.

  Design & Layout :
    тАв Rectangular, horizontally stacked text blocks.
    тАв Red and black colour scheme with white text for emphasis.
    тАв Bengali and English text combined for bilingual communication.
    тАв Wi-Fi icon suggests digital/online delivery.

  Dimensions & Placement :
    тАв "HSC 26" and subject list are in red rectangles; main batch name is in a larger black font.
    тАв Wi-Fi icon is placed at the upper right, aligned with the main text.

  Analysis :
    тАв The logo is designed to attract HSC 2026 candidates, highlighting online accessibility and coverage of three core subjects. The use of both Bengali and English text broadens its appeal to a diverse student base. <!-- figure, from page 17 (l=0.065,t=0.029,r=0.200,b=0.074), with ID 7b6e66ff-ac30-4208-9c26-5201b58a5ba9 -->

Summary : This is the logo for "10 Minute School", an educational platform, featuring stylized text and a graphic element.

logo: 10 Minute School

Logo Elements :
  тАв The number "10" is displayed in bold black font; the "0" is partially open at the top right.
  тАв A red arrow curves clockwise inside the "0", starting at the top left and ending at the top right, forming a partial circle.
  тАв The words "MINUTE SCHOOL" are written in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines to the right of the "10".
  тАв "MINUTE" is on the top line, "SCHOOL" is on the bottom line, both in a clean sans-serif font.

Dimensions & Placement :
  тАв The "10" and arrow graphic are left-aligned; the text is right-aligned to the graphic.
  тАв The red arrow is sized to fit neatly within the "0", visually connecting the number to the concept of time.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses a red arrow to symbolize the passage of time, reinforcing the "10 Minute" concept.
  тАв The clean, modern font and minimal color palette (black and red) convey a sense of professionalism and urgency appropriate for an educational brand focused on quick learning. <!-- figure, from page 17 (l=0.800,t=0.034,r=0.933,b=0.069), with ID 0d8771bd-8d4a-4c8b-8dee-bee896197e84 -->

logo: HSC 26 ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ (Bangla, English, ICT)
Summary : This is a logo for an online batch program targeting HSC 2026 students, with a focus on Bangla, English, and ICT subjects.

Logo Elements :
  тАв Main text: "HSC 26" in white font on a red background.
  тАв Secondary text: "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch in Bengali) in bold black Bengali script, with a wireless signal icon to the right.
  тАв Subtext: "ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ ┬╖ ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ ┬╖ ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐" (Bangla ┬╖ English ┬╖ ICT) in white font on a red background.
  тАв All text is horizontally aligned and uses a combination of Bengali and English.
  тАв The design uses red, black, and white as primary colours.

Dimensions & Placement :
  тАв Rectangular layout, with the main title at the top, followed by the Bengali script, and the subject list at the bottom.
  тАв Wireless signal icon is placed to the right of the main Bengali text.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo visually emphasizes the year "HSC 26" and the online nature of the batch with the wireless icon.
  тАв The use of both Bengali and English text targets a bilingual audience.
  тАв The red and black colour scheme is bold and attention-grabbing, suitable for educational branding. <!-- figure, from page 18 (l=0.065,t=0.028,r=0.199,b=0.075), with ID 4a463fb1-45aa-4407-b1fa-a8467bfc65bf -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text and Design :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" in bold black font, with the "0" partially open at the top right.
  тАв A red arrow curves clockwise inside the "0", forming part of the number and pointing to the right.
  тАв To the right of the "10", the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines: "MINUTE" on top, "SCHOOL" below.
  тАв The font is modern and sans-serif.
  тАв The logo is on a white background.

Dimensions and Placement :
  тАв The "10" is larger and positioned to the left, with "MINUTE SCHOOL" aligned vertically to its right.
  тАв The red arrow is integrated into the "0" and is a distinctive visual element.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses a bold, modern design with a red arrow to suggest speed or progress, aligning with the "10 Minute School" brand identity focused on quick learning. <!-- figure, from page 18 (l=0.801,t=0.034,r=0.932,b=0.069), with ID ece6e6de-d7e2-434d-b641-a4d5641ae4f7 -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Summary : This is the official logo of "10 Minute School", an educational platform.

Logo Elements :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" in bold black font.
  тАв The "0" in "10" is stylized with a red arrow forming part of the zero, pointing to the right and upward.
  тАв To the right of the number, the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines.
  тАв "MINUTE" is on the top line, "SCHOOL" is on the bottom line, both in a clean sans-serif font.
  тАв The overall design is horizontal, with the number and text aligned.

Dimensions & Placement :
  тАв The number "10" is approximately the same height as the stacked text.
  тАв The red arrow within the "0" is prominent and visually distinct.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses a bold, modern typeface and a red accent to draw attention.
  тАв The red arrow suggests progress, speed, or forward movement, aligning with the "10 Minute" concept of quick learning.
  тАв The clean design and clear text make the logo easily recognizable and suitable for digital platforms. <!-- figure, from page 19 (l=0.801,t=0.034,r=0.933,b=0.069), with ID 7cc0e2c3-befa-4530-812d-9bb30aadc80b -->

logo: HSC 26 ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ (Bangla, English, ICT)
Summary : This is a logo for an online batch program targeting HSC 2026 students, with a focus on Bangla, English, and ICT subjects.

Text Elements : 
  тАв "HSC 26" in bold white text on a red background.
  тАв "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch in Bengali) in bold black text.
  тАв "ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ тАв ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ тАв ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐" (Bangla тАв English тАв ICT) in white text on a red background.

Design Features : 
  тАв Red and black color scheme.
  тАв Wireless signal icon to the right of the main text, suggesting online connectivity.
  тАв Rectangular blocks for emphasis behind key text elements.

Dimensions & Placement : 
  тАв Horizontal layout with stacked text blocks.
  тАв All text is centered and aligned for clarity.

Analysis : 
  тАв The logo uses strong color contrast and clear subject focus to appeal to students preparing for the HSC 2026 exams, emphasizing online learning and the three core subjects. <!-- figure, from page 23 (l=0.064,t=0.028,r=0.199,b=0.075), with ID 4ced2abf-d34f-4dde-a296-16ca73cbba54 -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text and Design :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" in bold black font, with the "0" partially open and containing a red arrow curving clockwise inside it.
  тАв To the right of the "10", the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines ("MINUTE" above "SCHOOL").
  тАв The red arrow within the "0" visually suggests the passage of time or a clock motif.

Dimensions and Placement :
  тАв The "10" is positioned to the left, with the text "MINUTE SCHOOL" aligned to its right.
  тАв The design is horizontally oriented, with all elements on a white background.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses a red arrow to emphasize the concept of time, aligning with the "10 Minute" theme.
  тАв The clean, modern font and simple color palette (black and red) convey a professional and educational brand identity. <!-- figure, from page 23 (l=0.801,t=0.034,r=0.932,b=0.070), with ID 3cdb0f8c-6f17-4347-b6fd-3a6ea2902c21 -->

Summary : This is a logo for an online educational batch targeting HSC 2026 students, with text in both English and Bengali, and a focus on Bangla, English, and ICT subjects.

logo: HSC 26 Online Batch (ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ)
  Text Elements :
    тАв "HSC 26" in bold white text on a red background.
    тАв "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch in Bengali) in bold black text with a Wi-Fi signal icon.
    тАв "ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ ┬╖ ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ ┬╖ ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐" (Bangla ┬╖ English ┬╖ ICT) in white text on a red background.
  Design & Layout :
    тАв Rectangular, horizontally stacked text blocks.
    тАв Red and black colour scheme with white text for emphasis.
    тАв Wi-Fi signal icon to the right of the main Bengali text, suggesting online connectivity.
    тАв All text is centered and uses bold, sans-serif fonts.
  Dimensions & Placement :
    тАв "HSC 26" and subject list are in red rectangles; main Bengali text is in a larger black font.
    тАв Wi-Fi icon is placed at the upper right of the main text block.
  Analysis :
    тАв The logo is designed to attract HSC 2026 students to an online batch, emphasizing digital learning and coverage of three core subjects. The use of both English and Bengali broadens accessibility. <!-- figure, from page 25 (l=0.065,t=0.029,r=0.199,b=0.075), with ID 11c5542c-119f-441e-93ab-0f721c0e7053 -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text : 
  тАв "10 MINUTE SCHOOL" in uppercase letters.
  тАв "10" is stylized: the "1" is a black vertical bar, the "0" is a black circle with a red arrow forming part of the circle.

Design Elements : 
  тАв The "0" in "10" incorporates a red arrow curving clockwise, suggesting movement or progress.
  тАв Font is modern and sans-serif, with "10" larger than the rest of the text.
  тАв All text is black except for the red arrow.

Dimensions & Placement : 
  тАв "10" is on the left, with "MINUTE SCHOOL" stacked to the right in two lines.
  тАв "MINUTE" is above "SCHOOL", both right-aligned with the "10".

Analysis : 
  тАв The logo uses a red arrow to symbolize speed or forward motion, aligning with the "10 Minute" concept of quick learning.
  тАв The clean, modern design suggests a focus on education and accessibility. <!-- figure, from page 25 (l=0.801,t=0.035,r=0.932,b=0.069), with ID 1cab0705-876b-4ed1-9384-2e802b54a45d -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text and Design :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" in bold black font, with the "0" partially open and containing a red arrow curving clockwise inside it.
  тАв To the right of the number, the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines.
  тАв The red arrow within the "0" visually suggests the concept of time or a clock.

Dimensions and Placement :
  тАв The "10" is on the left, with "MINUTE SCHOOL" aligned to the right in two lines.
  тАв The red arrow is positioned inside the "0" and points upward and to the right.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses a simple, modern design with a red accent to draw attention to the concept of time, reinforcing the brand's focus on quick, efficient learning. <!-- figure, from page 29 (l=0.801,t=0.034,r=0.932,b=0.069), with ID 87311c8b-6289-4858-a23f-48a14d90280c -->

Summary : This is a logo for an online batch program targeting HSC 2026 students, with a focus on Bangla, English, and ICT subjects.

  тАв "HSC 26" in bold white text on a red background.
  тАв "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch in Bengali) in bold black text.
  тАв "ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ ┬╖ ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ ┬╖ ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐" (Bangla ┬╖ English ┬╖ ICT) in white text on a red background.
  тАв Wi-Fi signal icon to the right of the main text.

Design & Layout :
  тАв Rectangular, horizontally stacked text blocks.
  тАв Red and black color scheme with white text for emphasis.
  тАв Wi-Fi icon suggests online/virtual learning.

Dimensions & Placement :
  тАв All text is horizontally aligned and centered.
  тАв Wi-Fi icon is placed at the upper right of the main text block.

  тАв The logo uses bold colors and clear subject labels to target HSC 2026 students for online courses in Bangla, English, and ICT, emphasizing accessibility and digital delivery. <!-- figure, from page 34 (l=0.065,t=0.028,r=0.198,b=0.075), with ID 32035bfc-b2d9-4cdc-9adf-0ccc200b6338 -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text and Design :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" in bold black font, with the "0" partially open at the top right, forming a clockwise red arrow.
  тАв To the right of the number, the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines.
  тАв The red arrow within the "0" visually suggests the concept of time or a clock, reinforcing the "minute" theme.

Dimensions and Placement :
  тАв The "10" is on the left, with "MINUTE SCHOOL" aligned to the right in two lines.
  тАв The red arrow is integrated into the "0" of "10", pointing to the right.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses a red arrow to symbolize speed, progress, or the passage of time, aligning with the brand's focus on quick, efficient learning.

logo: 10 Minute School

Scene Overview : 
  тАв The image is a logo for "10 Minute School".
  тАв The design features a stylized "10" where the "1" is a simple black vertical line and the "0" is a black circle with a red arrow forming the upper right quadrant, resembling a clock hand pointing at 2 o'clock.

  тАв The colour palette is black for the text and circle, and red for the arrow.

  тАв No scale bar or additional UI elements are present.
  тАв The logo is horizontally oriented with the graphic on the left and text on the right.

  тАв The "10" is left-aligned, with the text block forming a right-aligned rectangle.
  тАв The red arrow within the "0" draws attention to the concept of time.

ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ
ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ тАв ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ тАв ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐ <!-- marginalia, from page 41 (l=0.065,t=0.029,r=0.200,b=0.075), with ID b405365e-0f30-4237-bb16-94990cbbbb7f -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text and Design :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" in bold black font, with the "0" partially open and featuring a red arrow forming part of the zero.
  тАв To the right of the number, the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines.
  тАв The red arrow within the "0" points to the right, suggesting forward movement or progress.

Dimensions and Placement :
  тАв The "10" is on the left, with "MINUTE SCHOOL" aligned to the right in two lines.
  тАв The red arrow is integrated into the "0" of "10", occupying the upper left quadrant of the zero.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses a bold, modern typeface and a red accent to draw attention to the concept of quick learning or progress, aligning with the brand's focus on short, effective educational content. <!-- figure, from page 41 (l=0.800,t=0.034,r=0.933,b=0.069), with ID c7ce3301-d00d-4d91-80de-d0c24aaa3a12 -->

Summary : This is a logo for an HSC 26 online batch program, with text in both English and Bengali, indicating subjects covered.

logo: HSC 26 Online Batch  
Visible Text : 
  тАв "HSC 26" in white text on a red background.
  тАв "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Bengali for "Online Batch") in bold black Bengali script.
  тАв "ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ тАв ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ тАв ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐" (Bengali for "Bangla тАв English тАв ICT") in white text on a red background.
  тАв A stylized wireless signal icon to the right of the main text.

Design Elements : 
  тАв Uses red, black, and white as primary colours.
  тАв Rectangular blocks for emphasis behind "HSC 26" and subject list.
  тАв Bengali and English text combined for bilingual communication.
  тАв Wireless signal icon suggests online or digital delivery.

Dimensions & Placement : 
  тАв Horizontal layout, with text and icons centered.
  тАв "HSC 26" and subject list are each on their own red background strips.

Analysis : 
  тАв The logo is designed to promote an online batch for HSC 2026 students, specifically for Bangla, English, and ICT subjects, using bold colours and bilingual text to attract attention and convey digital accessibility. <!-- figure, from page 42 (l=0.064,t=0.028,r=0.201,b=0.075), with ID a19cb245-0de3-440f-9b95-32aca24eb86c -->

Summary : This image is a logo for "10 Minute School," featuring stylized text and a graphic element.

logo: 10 Minute School

Logo Elements : 
  тАв The logo consists of the text "10 MINUTE SCHOOL."
  тАв The "10" is stylized: the "1" is a simple black vertical line, and the "0" is a black circle with a red arrow forming the upper left quadrant, pointing rightward.
  тАв "MINUTE SCHOOL" is written in uppercase, sans-serif font, in black.
  тАв The red arrow in the "0" visually suggests movement or progress, possibly referencing the "minute" or time aspect.

Dimensions & Placement : 
  тАв The "10" is on the left, with "MINUTE SCHOOL" stacked to the right in two lines.
  тАв The red arrow is integrated into the "0" of "10," making it distinctive.

  тАв The logo uses a minimalistic design with a red accent to draw attention to the concept of time and progress, aligning with the brand's educational focus on quick learning. <!-- figure, from page 42 (l=0.801,t=0.034,r=0.932,b=0.069), with ID e73610de-c8c7-402f-b97b-f48b40940290 -->

logo: HSC 26 ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ (Bangla, English, ICT)
Summary : This is a logo for an online batch program targeting HSC 2026 students, with a focus on Bangla, English, and ICT subjects.

Text Elements :
  тАв "HSC 26" in bold white text on a red background.
  тАв "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch in Bengali) in bold black text.
  тАв "ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ тАв ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ тАв ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐" (Bangla тАв English тАв ICT) in white text on a red background.

Design & Layout :
  тАв Rectangular, horizontally stacked text blocks.
  тАв Red and black color scheme with white text for contrast.
  тАв Wireless signal icon to the right of the main text, indicating online/virtual nature.

Dimensions & Placement :
  тАв All text is center-aligned.
  тАв Wireless icon is placed at the upper right of the main text block.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses bold colors and clear bilingual text to target Bangladeshi HSC students for an online batch, emphasizing the three core subjects and the digital/online delivery mode. <!-- figure, from page 43 (l=0.065,t=0.028,r=0.199,b=0.075), with ID 946b5bc6-f4e6-48aa-9e4f-c5f0a4e7b534 -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text & Design :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" in bold black font, with the "0" partially open at the top right.
  тАв A red arrow curves clockwise inside the "0", forming part of the number and pointing to the right.
  тАв To the right of the number, the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines: "MINUTE" above "SCHOOL".
  тАв The font is sans-serif and modern, with all elements aligned horizontally.

Dimensions & Placement :
  тАв The "10" and arrow are on the left, with "MINUTE SCHOOL" to the right.
  тАв The logo is rectangular, wider than tall, with the text occupying the right two-thirds.

Analysis :
  тАв The red arrow within the "0" visually suggests speed or movement, reinforcing the "10 Minute" concept of quick learning.
  тАв The clean, modern design and use of black and red create a professional and energetic impression. <!-- figure, from page 43 (l=0.801,t=0.034,r=0.931,b=0.069), with ID 717c279a-d109-444b-8664-a433ac465073 -->

Summary : This is a logo for an online educational batch targeting HSC 26 students, with a focus on Bangla, English, and ICT subjects.

logo:  
Visible Text & Elements :  
  тАв "HSC 26" in bold white text on a red background.  
  тАв "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch in Bengali) in bold black text.  
  тАв "ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ тАв ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ тАв ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐" (Bangla тАв English тАв ICT) in white text on a red background.  
  тАв Wi-Fi signal icon to the right of the main text, indicating online connectivity.

Design & Layout :  
  тАв Rectangular layout with red and black as primary colours.  
  тАв Text is arranged in three distinct sections: top (HSC 26), middle (main batch name), bottom (subject focus).  
  тАв Wi-Fi icon is placed to the right of the main batch name, suggesting digital/online learning.

Dimensions & Placement :  
  тАв All text is horizontally aligned and centered.  
  тАв The logo is compact, with each section clearly separated by background colour.

Analysis :  
  тАв The logo uses red to draw attention to the batch year and subject focus, while black is used for the main title for emphasis.  
  тАв The Wi-Fi icon reinforces the online nature of the batch.  
  тАв The inclusion of subject names highlights the academic focus areas. <!-- figure, from page 44 (l=0.065,t=0.029,r=0.200,b=0.075), with ID 33d19bb9-e4b1-47db-832f-4a143573d10e -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text and Design :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" in bold black font, with the "0" partially open and containing a red arrow curving clockwise inside it.
  тАв To the right of the number, the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines.
  тАв The design is simple, with a modern sans-serif typeface and a red accent for the arrow.

Dimensions and Placement :
  тАв The "10" is on the left, with "MINUTE" on the top right and "SCHOOL" directly below it.
  тАв The red arrow is integrated into the "0" of "10", pointing to the right.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses a red arrow to suggest speed or progress, aligning with the "10 Minute" concept of quick learning.
  тАв The clean, bold design emphasizes clarity and modernity, suitable for an educational platform. <!-- figure, from page 44 (l=0.801,t=0.034,r=0.932,b=0.069), with ID c6036487-047f-43fb-ab2e-97d4ef5b150c -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text and Design :
  тАв The logo consists of the text "10 MINUTE SCHOOL".
  тАв The "10" is stylized: the "1" is a simple black vertical line, and the "0" is a black circle with a red arrow forming part of its upper right quadrant.
  тАв "MINUTE" is written in uppercase black letters to the right of the "10".
  тАв "SCHOOL" is written in uppercase black letters below "MINUTE", aligned to the right.
  тАв The red arrow in the "0" points to the right, suggesting forward movement or progress.

Dimensions and Placement :
  тАв The logo is horizontally oriented, with "10" on the left and the stacked "MINUTE SCHOOL" on the right.
  тАв The red arrow is integrated into the "0" of "10", occupying the upper right quadrant.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo uses a bold, modern sans-serif font and a red accent to convey energy and urgency, aligning with the "10 Minute" concept of quick learning.

Summary : This is a logo for an online educational batch targeting HSC 26 students, with a focus on Bangla, English, and ICT subjects.

logo: HSC 26 Online Batch (ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ тАв ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ тАв ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐)

    тАв Main subject is the text "HSC 26 ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch) with a Wi-Fi signal icon, indicating an online learning platform.
    тАв Subtext in red highlights the subjects: "ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ тАв ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ тАв ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐" (Bangla, English, ICT).
    тАв The design uses bold black and red text on a white background for high contrast and visibility.
  Technical Details :
    тАв "HSC 26" and the subject list are in white text on red rectangular backgrounds.
    тАв "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" is in large, bold black Bengali script.
    тАв Wi-Fi signal icon to the right of the main text, suggesting online connectivity.
  Spatial Relationships :

    тАв The subject list is centered below the main text, all elements aligned vertically.
  Analysis :
    тАв The logo uses red to draw attention to key information (batch year and subjects), while the Wi-Fi icon reinforces the online nature of the batch. ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ
ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ ┬╖ ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ ┬╖ ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐ <!-- marginalia, from page 47 (l=0.064,t=0.028,r=0.201,b=0.075), with ID 19c1c0de-4786-4c89-af30-e2a9c4bb58a1 -->

logo: 10 Minute School

Visible Text and Design :
  тАв The logo consists of the number "10" in bold black font, with the "0" partially open at the top right.
  тАв A red arrow curves clockwise inside the "0", forming part of the number and pointing to the right.
  тАв To the right of the "10", the words "MINUTE SCHOOL" appear in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines.
  тАв The design uses a clean, sans-serif typeface and a minimalistic color palette (black and red on white).

Dimensions and Placement :
  тАв The "10" is on the left, with "MINUTE SCHOOL" aligned to its right.
  тАв The red arrow is integrated into the "0" of "10", making it visually distinctive.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo visually emphasizes the concept of "10 minutes" with the arrow suggesting speed, progress, or a countdown, aligning with the brand's focus on quick, efficient learning. <!-- figure, from page 47 (l=0.801,t=0.034,r=0.932,b=0.069), with ID 35d248ed-d2e7-4a13-acfa-b095375ec94d -->

Summary : This image is a logo for an online batch program targeting HSC 26 students, with content in Bangla, English, and ICT.

logo: HSC 26 Online Batch
  тАв Main text: "HSC 26" in white on a red background.
  тАв Large black Bengali text: "ржЕржирж▓рж╛ржЗржи ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЪ" (Online Batch).
  тАв Subtext in red: "ржмрж╛ржВрж▓рж╛ тАв ржЗржВрж░рзЗржЬрж┐ тАв ржЖржЗрж╕рж┐ржЯрж┐" (Bangla тАв English тАв ICT).
  тАв Wireless signal icon to the right of the main text.
  тАв Rectangular layout, high contrast with red, black, and white color scheme.

Analysis :
  тАв The logo is designed to be bold and easily recognizable, emphasizing the year (HSC 26) and the online nature of the batch. The inclusion of subject names in both Bengali and English highlights the program's academic focus. <!-- figure, from page 48 (l=0.065,t=0.028,r=0.200,b=0.075), with ID 07cc0151-8340-4727-b65c-05098eec07be -->

Summary : This image is a logo for "10 Minute School," featuring stylized text and a graphic element.

logo: 10 Minute School

Logo Elements :
  тАв The number "10" is displayed in bold black font.
  тАв The "0" in "10" contains a red arrow curving clockwise, forming part of the zero.
  тАв The words "MINUTE SCHOOL" are written in uppercase black letters, stacked in two lines to the right of the "10".
  тАв "MINUTE" is on the top line, "SCHOOL" is on the bottom line.
  тАв The font is modern and sans-serif.

Dimensions & Placement :
  тАв The "10" is on the left, with the text "MINUTE SCHOOL" aligned to the right.
  тАв The red arrow is positioned inside the "0" and points upward and to the right.

Analysis :
  тАв The red arrow within the "0" visually suggests the concept of time or a countdown, reinforcing the "10 Minute" theme of the brand.
